## 0. Research Metadata

이번 loop 227은 직전 L8 R13 세트(loop 224 Stage2 false-positive, loop 225 high-MAE, loop 226 4B/4C RedTeam)를 이어받는 네 번째 holdout이다. 새 C26/C27/C28 row 수를 늘리지 않고, 같은 source rows가 promotion evidence로 쓰일 만큼 source/evidence/trust quality를 갖췄는지 검증한다.

## 1. Current Calibrated Profile Assumption

current_default_profile_proxy = e2r_2_1_stock_web_calibrated / active selector = e2r_2_2 가정. 이번 MD는 production scoring 변경이 아니라 shadow-only R13 holdout이다.

## 3. Previous Coverage / Duplicate Avoidance Check

No-Repeat Index 원본에서 C26은 106 rows, C27은 48 rows, C28은 28 rows다. 직전 loop 224~226은 이 L8 source row 68개를 Stage2 false-positive, high-MAE, 4B/4C로 이미 검증했다. 따라서 이번 loop는 source Cxx coverage를 새로 주장하지 않고 `source_Cxx_coverage_mutated=false`로만 R13 price/evidence/trust validation을 수행한다.

## 7. Case Selection Summary

이 파일은 L8의 growth vocabulary를 한 번 더 의심한다. 플랫폼 매출, 글로벌 IP, cloud/security, AI partner, user count가 있어도 evidence URL이 없거나 source-proxy-only라면 red-team row로는 유효하지만 promotion evidence로는 부족하다. 반대로 retained-economics bridge와 price path가 동시에 맞은 control positive는 source 품질이 깨끗하다면 과잉 차단하지 않는다.

## 13. Current Calibrated Profile Stress Test

current_profile_error_count = 47. 가장 큰 residual은 URL/proxy quality가 약한 row가 retained-economics bridge 없이 Stage2 후보처럼 보이는 것이다. 가격은 계산됐지만 evidence ledger가 약하면 promotion input으로 쓰면 안 된다.

## 14. Stage2 / Yellow / Green Comparison

R13 holdout이므로 신규 Green unlock은 하지 않는다. Stage2-Actionable은 `price_evidence_control_validated`와 깨끗한 source row에만 남기고, source_proxy/url_missing/high-MAE row는 Stage2-Watch 또는 local 4B로 제한한다.

## 15. 4B Local vs Full-window Timing Audit

Loop 226의 4B/4C verdict를 가져와 source quality를 덧씌웠다. URL이 빈 event-cap row는 4B-watch로는 쓸 수 있지만 promotion evidence로는 금지한다.

## 16. 4C Protection Audit

L8 source rows에서 hard accounting trust break는 0개로 본다. Kakao·Com2uS·SGA솔루션즈 같은 trust/impairment/zero-trust 언어는 reviewable overhang으로 남기고, hard 4C는 retained-economics break나 second trust confirmation이 붙을 때만 허용한다.

## 17. Sector-Specific Rule Candidate

`L8_PRICE_EVIDENCE_SOURCE_TRUST_GATE_V4`: L8에서 growth vocabulary가 있더라도 evidence_url/source quality와 retained-economics bridge가 없으면 Stage2-Actionable promotion input으로 쓰지 않는다.

## 18. Canonical-Archetype Rule Candidate

`R13_PRICE_EVIDENCE_SOURCE_TRUST_VALIDATION_GATE_V4`: complete MFE/MAE row는 price validation에는 충분하지만 promotion validation에는 source URL, source-proxy replacement, second trust confirmation이 추가로 필요하다.

## 19. Before / After Backtest Comparison

| profile | change | expected effect |
|---|---|---|
| P0 | current proxy | retains existing mix of watch/actionable rows |
| P1 | retained-economics gate | lowers low-MFE/high-MAE false positives |
| P2 | source-quality gate | blocks URL-missing/proxy-only promotion |
| P3 | trust second-confirmation gate | avoids both premature hard 4C and blind promotion |

## 26. Deferred Coding Agent Handoff Prompt

### Purpose
You are now in the repository implementation phase. The attached Markdown files are v12 post-calibrated residual research outputs produced using the Songdaiki/stock-web OHLC atlas. These MDs are not live candidate research. They are historical calibration research designed to extend the already-applied e2r_2_1_stock_web_calibrated profile. Do not blindly apply every shadow row. Ingest the machine-readable rows and update the sector/canonical-archetype calibration ledger.

### Price source context
- Primary historical price source used by the research MD: Songdaiki/stock-web.
- Price basis: tradable_raw.
- Price adjustment status: raw_unadjusted_marcap.
- Price shard pattern: atlas/ohlcv_tradable_by_symbol_year/<prefix>/<ticker>/<year>.csv.
- Symbol profile pattern: atlas/symbol_profiles/<prefix>/<ticker>.json.

### Rules
- Use only calibration_usable=true rows for quantitative calibration.
- Do not count R13 holdout reused cases as new source Cxx coverage.
- Do not promote URL-missing or source-proxy-only rows without source repair.
- Hard 4C on trust/accounting requires second non-price confirmation unless price formation itself is invalidated.
- Production scoring must not change unless the user explicitly asks for another promotion batch.

### Expected repository tasks
1. Parse case / trigger / score_simulation / shadow_weight / residual_contribution rows.
2. Validate stock-web price source fields.
3. Validate R13 scope and source_Cxx_coverage_mutated=false.
4. Deduplicate same_entry_group_id.
5. Treat this file as R13 guardrail holdout, not new L8 coverage.
